## 李旭婷
---
## Chinese personal name
### Lǐ Xùtíng
---
- **definition:** Chinese personal name
- **pinyin:** Lǐ Xùtíng
- **components:**
  - 李
    - Lǐ
    - a common Chinese surname
  - 旭
    - xù
    - dawn; rising sun
  - 婷
    - tíng
    - graceful; elegant; attractive
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** A Chinese personal name, typically consisting of a family name followed by two given names.
  - **interpretation:** 李 (Lǐ, "a common Chinese surname") is one of the most common Chinese surnames, originating from the plum tree. 旭 (xù, "dawn; rising sun") represents the rising sun and often symbolizes new beginnings or hope. 婷 (tíng, "graceful; elegant; attractive") suggests grace and elegance. Together, the name 李旭婷 (Lǐ Xùtíng) combines the common surname 李 with a given name evoking the hopeful beauty of a new dawn and grace, typical for personal names that reflect positive attributes or aspirations for the individual.
- **examples:**
  - 李旭婷是我的好朋友。
    - Lǐ Xùtíng shì wǒ de hǎo péngyǒu.
    - Li Xuting is my good friend.
  - 我( )昨( )天( )见(見)到( )了( )李( )旭( )婷( )，她( )看( )起( )来(來)很( )开(開)心( )。
    - Wǒ zuótiān jiàn dào le Lǐ Xùtíng, tā kàn qǐlái hěn kāixīn.
    - I met Li Xuting yesterday, she looked very happy.
  - 李旭婷喜( )欢(歡)旅( )行( )，她( )去( )过(過)很( )多( )国(國)家( )。
    - Lǐ Xùtíng xǐhuān lǚxíng, tā qù guò hěn duō guójiā.
    - Li Xuting likes traveling, she has visited many countries.
### 李旭婷 → 李
- **definition:** a common Chinese surname
- **pinyin:** Lǐ
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 來 (lái, originally representing 'wheat') became corrupted to 木 (mù, 'tree') + semantic 子 (zǐ, 'child') ->
    - 李
  - **interpretation:** Originally a phono-semantic compound with 來 (lái, originally 'wheat') providing sound and 子 (zǐ, 'child') lending meaning. Over time, 來 was corrupted to 木 (mù, 'tree'), suggesting a 'plum tree', which is also associated with the surname Li, well-known in Chinese culture.
- **examples:**
  - 李( )老( )师(師)是( )我( )们(們)的( )数(數)学(學)老( )师(師)。
    - Lǐ lǎoshī shì wǒmen de shùxué lǎoshī.
    - Mr. Li is our math teacher.
  - 李( )先( )生( )邀( )请(請)我( )们(們)去( )他( )的( )茶( )馆(館)。
    - Lǐ xiānshēng yāoqǐng wǒmen qù tā de cháguǎn.
    - Mr. Li invited us to his tea house.
  - 我( )常( )常( )和( )李( )小( )姐( )去( )公( )园(園)散( )步( )。
    - Wǒ chángcháng hé Lǐ xiǎojiě qù gōngyuán sànbù.
    - I often go for walks in the park with Miss Li.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 李](@media/glyph674e.png)

  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把( )椅( )子( )的( )主( )要( )材( )料( )是( )木( )。

    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.

### 李旭婷 → 旭
- **definition:** dawn; rising sun
- **pinyin:** xù
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 九
    - jiǔ
    - nine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 日 (rì, "sun") + phonetic 九 (jiǔ) ->
    - rising sun
  - **interpretation:** The character 旭(xù, "rising sun; dawn") combines the semantic component 日 (rì, "sun"), suggesting brightness or a celestial body, with the phonetic component 九 (jiǔ), which contributes the sound. This combination conveys the sense of the sun rising, signifying dawn or the early morning.
- **examples:**
  - 天( )边(邊)露( )出( )了( )旭( )日( )，空( )气(氣)显(顯)得( )特( )别(別)清( )新( )。
    - Tiānbiān lùchūle xùrì, kōngqì xiǎnde tèbié qīngxīn.
    - The rising sun appeared on the horizon, and the air felt especially fresh.
  - 旭( )光( )渐(漸)渐(漸)照( )亮( )了( )大( )地( )。
    - Xù guāng jiànjiàn zhàoliàngle dàdì.
    - The light of the rising sun gradually illuminated the land.
  - 每( )天( )清( )晨( )，我( )们(們)都( )会(會)沐( )浴( )在( )旭( )日( )的( )光( )辉(輝)中( )。
    - Měitiān qīngchén, wǒmen dōu huì mùyù zài xù rì de guānghuī zhōng.
    - Every morning, we bathe in the glory of the rising sun.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 旭](@media/glyph65ed.png)
### 李旭婷 → 旭 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 李旭婷 → 旭 → 九
- **definition:** nine
- **pinyin:** jiǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized hand with bent wrist ->
    - original 'elbow' 肘 (zhǒu) meaning ->
    - associated with nine as metaphorical bumping up against ten
  - **interpretation:** 九 originally depicted the elbow, symbolizing movement akin to pulling back in momentum, which culturally reflects nearing a complete cycle at ten. Later, 九 came to symbolize the number nine, a fist bumping up against ten, the last count on one's fingers.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )是( )九( )号(號)。
    - Jīntiān shì jiǔ hào.
    - Today is the ninth.
  - 她( )有( )九( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Tā yǒu jiǔ gè píngguǒ.
    - She has nine apples.
  - 我( )们(們)九( )点(點)钟(鐘)出( )发(發)，去探望朋友。
    - Wǒmen jiǔ diǎn zhōng chūfā, qù tànwàng péngyǒu.
    - We will leave at nine o'clock to visit a friend.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 九](@media/glyph4e5d.png)
### 李旭婷 → 婷
- **definition:** graceful; elegant; attractive
- **pinyin:** tíng
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
  - 亭
    - tíng
    - pavilion
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 女 (nǚ, "woman") + phonetic 亭 (tíng) ->
    - graceful, elegant
  - **interpretation:** The character uses 女 (nǚ, "woman") as its semantic component, indicating qualities typically associated with femininity, such as grace and elegance. 亭 (tíng) provides the phonetic component, contributing its sound to the character.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )的( )舞( )姿( )非( )常( )优(優)雅( )，如( )同( )一( )朵( )轻(輕)盈( )的( )莲(蓮)花( )。
    - Tā de wǔzī fēicháng yōuyǎ, rútóng yī duǒ qīngyíng de liánhuā.
    - Her dance moves are very graceful, like a light lotus flower.
  - 这(這)个(個)花( )园(園)设(設)计(計)得( )很( )精( )致(緻)，充( )满(滿)了( )优(優)雅( )的( )气(氣)息( )。
    - Zhège huāyuán shèjì de hěn jīngzhì, chōngmǎn le yōuyǎ de qìxī.
    - This garden is designed meticulously and is filled with an elegant ambiance.
  - 她( )散( )发(發)着(著)一( )种(種)自( )然( )的( )美( )丽(麗)，令( )人( )赞(讚)叹(嘆)不( )已( )。
    - Tā sànfā zhe yī zhǒng zìrán de měilì, lìngrén zàntàn bùyǐ.
    - She exudes a natural beauty that leaves people in awe.
### 李旭婷 → 婷 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )位( )才( )华(華)横(橫)溢( )的( )女( )，赢(贏)得( )了( )全( )场(場)注( )目( )。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古( )时(時)候( )‘女( )’常( )被( )用( )来(來)象( )征(徵)温(溫)柔( )，而( )如( )今( )它( )代( )表( )独(獨)立( )自( )信( )。

## 松茸
---
## matsutake mushroom
### sōng róng
---
- **definition:** matsutake mushroom
- **pinyin:** sōng róng
- **components:**
  - 松
    - sōng
    - pine
  - 茸
    - róng
    - mushroom; fungi; soft growth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 松 (sōng, "pine") refers to the tree species and is often associated with natural or wild environments. 茸 (róng, "mushroom") is used to denote soft, downy growths or fungi such as mushrooms.
  - **interpretation:** 松茸 (sōngróng, "matsutake mushroom") refers to a type of mushroom known for growing in pine forests. The name emphasizes the natural habitat of the matsutake, which is often found among pine trees.
- **examples:**
  - 松( )茸( )是( )一( )种(種)名( )贵(貴)的( )食( )用( )菌( )。
    - sōng róng shì yī zhǒng míng guì de shí yòng jūn.
    - Matsutake mushroom is a prized edible fungus.
  - 松( )茸( )在( )深( )山( )中( )生( )长(長)，被( )誉(譽)为(為)珍( )稀( )食( )品( )。
    - sōng róng zài shēn shān zhōng shēng zhǎng, bèi yù wéi zhēn xī shí pǐn.
    - Matsutake mushrooms grow in deep mountains and are revered as a rare delicacy.
### 松茸 → 松(鬆)
- **traditional:** 鬆
- **definition:** pine
- **pinyin:** sōng
- **components:**
  - 髟
    - biāo
    - hair
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 髟 ("hair") + phonetic 松 (sōng) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** 鬆 (sōng, "loose") combines 髟 (biāo, "hair") as the semantic element expressing the idea of looseness or something flowing freely, similar to hair, with 松 (sōng, "pine") as the phonetic element. This links to the concept of being loose or relaxed, as hair can freely flow and pine branches are not tightly bound.
  - **simplification:** The simplified form 松(鬆) (sōng, "pine") retains 毛 (máo, "fur") as a reduced element replacing 髟 (biāo, "hair") and removing excess components for simplicity.
- **examples:**
  - 院( )子( )里(裡)有( )一( )棵( )高( )大( )的( )松(鬆)树(樹)。
    - Yuànzi lǐ yǒu yī kē gāodà de sōngshù.
    - There is a tall pine tree in the yard.
  - 那( )片( )森( )林( )以( )松(鬆)树(樹)闻(聞)名( )。
    - Nà piàn sēnlín yǐ sōngshù wénmíng.
    - That forest is famous for its pine trees.
  - 他( )躺( )在( )松(鬆)针(針)覆( )盖(蓋)的( )地( )面( )上( )。
    - Tā tǎng zài sōngzhēn fùgài de dìmiàn shàng.
    - He lay on the ground covered with pine needles.
### 松茸 → 松(鬆) → 髟
- **definition:** hair
- **pinyin:** biāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person with long hair ->
    - represents long hair
  - **interpretation:** The character 髟(biāo, "hair") is a pictogram, symbolizing a person adorned with long hair, emphasizing its characteristic texture and appearance.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )的( )髟( )柔( )顺(順)如( )丝(絲)。
    - Tā de biāo róushùn rú sī.
    - Her hair is as smooth as silk.
  - 他( )每( )天( )早( )上( )花( )时(時)间(間)整( )理( )髟( )，保( )持( )整( )洁(潔)。
    - Tā měitiān zǎoshang huā shíjiān zhěnglǐ biāo, bǎochí zhěngjié.
    - He spends time every morning tidying his hair, keeping it neat.
  - 这(這)本( )字( )典( )详(詳)细(細)介( )绍(紹)了( )髟( )的( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Zhè běn zìdiǎn xiángxì jièshào le biāo de lìshǐ.
    - This dictionary details the history of the hair radical.

### 松茸 → 茸
- **definition:** mushroom; fungi; soft growth
- **pinyin:** róng
- **components:**
  - 艸
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 聰
    - cōng
    - intelligent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艸 ('grass') + phonetic abbreviation of 聰 ('intelligent') ->
    - fungi/mushroom
  - **interpretation:** The character 茸(róng) ('mushroom; fungi; soft growth') combines 艸 (cǎo, 'grass') as the semantic component, indicating the natural plant-like or soft qualities of fungi, with a phonetic abbreviation from 聰 (cōng, 'intelligent'). The phonetic part contributes the sound, while the semantic part relates to the character's meaning of something growing among or resembling grass, like fungi or soft growth.
- **examples:**
  - 草( )原( )上( )长(長)满(滿)了( )茸( )草( )。
    - Cǎoyuán shàng zhǎng mǎn le róngcǎo.

    - Her teddy bear has a fluffy surface.

    - Shùlín lǐ chōngmǎn le gè zhǒng gè yàng de róng.
    - The forest is filled with various types of fungi.
### 松茸 → 茸 → 艸
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - grass
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts grass blades ->
    - duplication of 屮 (chè, 'grass') ->
    - grass imagery
  - **interpretation:** The character 艸(cǎo, 'grass') is a pictorial representation of grass blades. It is essentially a duplication of the character 屮 (chè, 'grass'), visually suggesting the appearance of grass tufts through repetition, emphasizing the concept of grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 公( )园(園)里(裡)绿(綠)艸( )茵( )茵( )。
    - Gōngyuán lǐ lǜ cǎo yīn yīn.

    - Chénlù zīrùn cǎo cóng, wēifēng shǐ tāmen qǐwǔ.
    - The morning dew nourishes the cluster of grass, and the breeze makes them dance.
  - 秋( )天( )时(時)艸( )变(變)黄(黃)，冬天它又枯萎。
    - Qiūtiān shí cǎo biàn huáng, dōngtiān tā yòu kūwěi.
    - In autumn, the grass turns yellow, and in winter, it withers.

### 松茸 → 茸 → 艸 → 屮
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)后(後)，小( )屮( )冲(沖)破( )泥( )土( )而( )出( )。

    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.

### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰
- **definition:** intelligent
- **pinyin:** cōng
- **components:**
  - 耳
    - ěr
    - ear
  - 悤
    - cōng
    - intelligent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 耳 (ěr, "ear") + phonetic 悤 (cōng) ->
    - listening ear leading to intelligence
  - **interpretation:** The character 聰(cōng, "clever") represents the concept of intelligence through sensitivity to sound and willingness to listen. The semantic component 耳 (ěr, "ear") signifies listening, while the phonetic component 悤 (cōng) helps convey the sound. Together, they depict someone who is keen at understanding and learning via hearing, reflecting cleverness.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )很( )聪(聰)明( )，总(總)是( )能( )找( )到( )解( )决(決)问(問)题(題)的( )方( )法( )。

    - He is very clever and always finds ways to solve problems.

    - Cōngmíng de rén tōngcháng hěn yǒu chuàngyì.
    - Clever people are often very creative.
  - 这(這)本( )书(書)适(適)合( )聪(聰)明( )的( )学(學)生( )阅(閱)读(讀)。
    - Zhè běn shū shìhé cōngmíng de xuéshēng yuèdú.

### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 耳
- **definition:** ear
- **pinyin:** ěr
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an ear
  - **interpretation:** The character 耳 (ěr, "ear") is a pictogram that visually represents an ear with its distinctive shape. This straightforward representation made it intuitive for ancient speakers to associate the character directly with the concept of an ear.
- **examples:**
  - 音( )乐(樂)直( )入( )耳( )。
    - Yīn yuè zhí rù ěr.
    - The music goes straight to the ear.

    - Tā qīn ěr tīng dào yáo yán, xīn zhōng chōng mǎn yí lǜ.

### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 悤
- **definition:** intelligent
- **pinyin:** cōng
- **components:**
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
  - 囪
    - cōng
    - patterned shape
  - 聰
    - cōng
    - intelligent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 心 (xīn, "heart") + 囪 as a patterned shape in Han dynasty ->
    - evolved from original cleverness ->
    - later indicating haste
  - **interpretation:** The original form of 悤 (cōng, "clever") depicts a heart 心 (xīn, "heart") with a dot indicating a hole, which symbolized intelligence. Over time, the dot evolved into a more complex pattern 囪 during the Han dynasty, transforming the character's meaning to indicate haste, possibly due to the idea of learning quickly or acting with intelligence. This semantic shift is reflected in its derivation to 聰 (cōng, "intelligent") that preserves the original meaning of cleverness.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 悤](@media/glyph60a4.png)
### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 悤 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一( )直( )都( )在( )帮(幫)助( )别(別)人( )。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有( )一( )个(個)美( )丽(麗)的( )公( )园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多( )人( )来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.

### 松茸 → 茸 → 聰 → 悤 → 囪
- **definition:** patterned shape
- **pinyin:** cōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a window with a shutter ->
    - original representation of an architectural feature
  - **interpretation:** The character 囪(cōng, 'patterned shape') originally depicted a window closed with a shutter, visually representing an architectural feature that provided ventilation and light while maintaining security. This representation suggests the utility and style of such windows, forming the basis for its association with patterns or shapes.

## 油( )条(條)
---
## fried dough stick
### yóu tiáo
---
- **traditional:** 油條
- **definition:** fried dough stick
- **pinyin:** yóu tiáo
- **components:**
  - 油
    - yóu
    - oil
  - 条(條)
    - tiáo
    - strip; streak; item
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 油 (yóu, "oil") + 条(條) (tiáo, "strip") =
    - 油( )条(條) (yóutiáo, "fried dough stick")
  - **interpretation:** The term refers to a strip of dough that is deep-fried in oil, common in Chinese cuisine as a breakfast item or snack. The name directly describes its preparation method and shape: frying (油) in oil and its oblong, strip-like form (条).
  - **simplification:** Simplified from 油條
- **examples:**
  - 早( )餐( )常( )常( )配( )有( )油( )条(條)和( )豆( )浆(漿)。
    - Zǎocān chángcháng pèiyǒu yóutiáo hé dòujiāng.
    - Breakfast is often served with fried dough sticks and soy milk.
  - 中( )式( )早( )餐( )里(裡)有( )油( )条(條)，口( )感( )松( )软(軟)细(細)腻(膩)。
    - Zhōngshì zǎocān lǐ yǒu yóutiáo, kǒugǎn sōngruǎn xìnì.
    - In Chinese-style breakfasts, fried dough sticks are present, and they have a soft and delicate texture.
  - 唐( )代( )的( )市( )集( )常( )见(見)油( )条(條)，深( )受( )市( )民( )喜( )爱(愛)。
    - Tángdài de shìjí chángjiàn yóutiáo, shēnshòu shìmín xǐ'ài.
    - In the Tang Dynasty markets, fried dough sticks were commonly seen and were much loved by citizens.
### 油( )条(條) → 油
- **definition:** oil
- **pinyin:** yóu
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 由
    - yóu
    - reason
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵 (shuǐ, 'water') + phonetic 由 (yóu, 'reason') =
    - liquid that flows ->
    - oil, sauce
  - **interpretation:** The character 油(yóu) combines the water radical 氵 (shuǐ, 'water') with the phonetic 由 (yóu, 'reason'). This suggests something liquid, aligning with the meanings 'oil' and 'sauce', both of which flow like water.
- **examples:**
  - 油( )可( )以( )用( )来(來)炒( )菜( )。
    - Yóu kěyǐ yòng lái chǎo cài.
    - Oil can be used for stir-frying dishes.
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)辣( )椒( )油( )，因( )为(為)它( )增( )加( )了( )味( )道( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān làjiāo yóu, yīnwèi tā zēngjiāle wèidào.
    - I like chili oil because it enhances the flavor.
  - 煎( )鱼(魚)时(時)可( )以( )先( )在( )鱼(魚)上( )抹( )点(點)油( )，这(這)样(樣)鱼(魚)更( )滑( )嫩( )。
    - Jiān yú shí kěyǐ xiān zài yú shàng mǒ diǎn yóu, zhèyàng yú gèng huá nèn.
    - When pan-frying fish, you can first spread a little oil on the fish, so that the fish becomes more tender.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 油](@media/glyph6cb9.png)
### 油( )条(條) → 油 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )偏( )旁( )氵( )，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快( )戏(戲)水( )。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 油( )条(條) → 油 → 由
- **definition:** reason
- **pinyin:** yóu
- **components:**
  - 十
    - shí
    - ten
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 十 (needle) + semantic 口 (mouth) ->
    - container with a needle symbolizing an ancient pronunciation
  - **interpretation:** The character 由(yóu, 'cause') depicts a container with a top resembling a needle (十), phonetic for sound with 口 (mouth) for semantic influence, symbolizing something that originates from a cause, just as contents originate from a container.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)问(問)题(題)由( )他( )负(負)责(責)。
    - Zhège wèntí yóu tā fùzé.
    - This issue is caused by him to be responsible.
  - 一( )切( )的( )变(變)化( )都( )是( )由( )时(時)间(間)引( )起( )的( )。
    - Yīqiè de biànhuà dōu shì yóu shíjiān yǐnqǐ de.
    - All changes are caused by the passage of time.
  - 胜(勝)利( )由( )努( )力( )而( )来(來)。
    - Shènglì yóu nǔlì ér lái.
    - Victory is caused by effort.

### 油( )条(條) → 油 → 由 → 十
- **definition:** ten
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original vertical stroke ->
    - later horizontal stroke added ->
    - forms a cross ->
    - represents 'ten'
  - **interpretation:** The character 十(shí, 'ten') represents the number ten with a cross shape that could be seen as tally marks. It evolved from a simple vertical stroke to a cross by adding a horizontal stroke, symbolizing a complete set of ten.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )十( )本( )书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu shí běn shū.
    - I have ten books.
  - 花( )园(園)里(裡)有( )十( )棵( )树(樹)，景( )色( )十( )分( )优(優)美( )。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu shí kē shù, jǐngsè shífēn yōuměi.
    - There are ten trees in the garden, and the scenery is very beautiful.
  - 十( )年( )磨( )一( )剑(劍)。
    - Shí nián mó yī jiàn.
    - It takes ten years of practice to hone a sword.

### 油( )条(條) → 油 → 由 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

### 油( )条(條) → 条(條)
- **traditional:** 條
- **definition:** strip; streak; item
- **pinyin:** tiáo
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 攸
    - yōu
    - a place far away
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood") + phonetic 攸 (yōu) ->
    - originally indicates a small branch or wooden stick
  - **interpretation:** The character 條 (tiáo, "strip; streak; item") combines the semantic 木 (mù, "wood") to suggest something made of wood, and the phonetic 攸 (yōu) to provide the pronunciation. Initially, it referred specifically to a small branch or stick made of wood, which logically leads to the modern extended meanings of a 'strip' or 'item' in more general contexts because of the similar shape and form.
  - **simplification:** 条(條) simplifies 條 by removing the 木 (mù, "wood") component and simplifying 攸 (yōu) to a simpler form, focusing on phonetics rather than semantic resemblance to wood.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)裙( )子( )很( )好( )看( )。
    - Zhè tiáo qúnzi hěn hǎokàn.
    - This dress looks very nice.
  - 河( )上( )架( )了( )一( )座( )长(長)长(長)的( )桥(橋)。
    - Hé shàng jiàle yī zuò cháng cháng de qiáo.
    - A long bridge was built over the river.
  - 他( )发(發)送( )了( )一( )条(條)短( )信( )，通( )知( )朋( )友( )聚( )会(會)时(時)间(間)。
    - Tā fāsòngle yī tiáo duǎnxìn, tōngzhī péngyǒu jùhuì shíjiān.
    - He sent a text message, informing friends of the gathering time.
### 油( )条(條) → 条(條) → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把( )椅( )子( )的( )主( )要( )材( )料( )是( )木( )。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.

### 油( )条(條) → 条(條) → 攸
- **definition:** a place far away
- **pinyin:** yōu
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 攴
    - pū
    - strike
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 攴 (pū, "strike" or "hit") ->
    - depiction may include drops of water ->
    - combines to suggest 'warning' or 'purification'
  - **interpretation:** The character 攸 is an ideogrammic compound with 人 (rén, "person") + 攴 (pū, "strike" or "hit"). Two interpretations exist: one posits it as a depiction of a person about to be disciplined, thus suggesting 'warning'; another suggests a ritual washing, connected to ceremonial purification, and thus involves water symbolism. The sense of 'distant' likely emerged as a metaphorical extension from the idea of warning or cleansing, which sets one apart or corrects a path.
- **historical forms:**

### 油( )条(條) → 条(條) → 攸 → 攴

  - 又
    - yòu

  - 卜
    - bǔ

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**

  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.

## 海派
---
## Shanghai style
### hǎi pài
---
- **definition:** Shanghai style
- **pinyin:** hǎi pài
- **components:**
  - 海
    - hǎi
    - sea; ocean; maritime; large
  - 派
    - pài
    - style; group; faction; school
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 海 (hǎi, "sea") refers to the coastal and maritime element of Shanghai, a city near the East China Sea, indicating the openness and cosmopolitan nature of the city due to its sea connections. 派 (pài, "style; school; faction") describes a distinct approach or characteristic appearance related to a group or region. Here, it indicates a distinctive style that is associated with Shanghai.
  - **interpretation:** 海 (hǎi, "sea") suggests the openness, trade, and external influences due to Shanghai's maritime location, reflecting a cosmopolitan lifestyle. 派 (pài, "style; school") implies a unique cultural or artistic expression, and in this context, refers to the innovative and avant-garde aspects of Shanghai's culture and lifestyle shaped by its international interactions.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )穿( )着(著)非( )常( )海( )派( )。
    - Tā de chuānzhuó fēicháng hǎi pài.
    - His clothing style is very Shanghai style.
  - 这(這)种(種)建( )筑(築)体(體)现(現)了( )海( )派( )风(風)格( )。
    - Zhè zhǒng jiànzhù tǐxiànle hǎi pài fēnggé.
    - This type of architecture embodies the Shanghai style.
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)海( )派( )的( )艺(藝)术(術)作( )品( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān hǎi pài de yìshù zuòpǐn.
    - I love Shanghai style art pieces.
### 海派 → 海
- **definition:** sea; ocean; maritime; large
- **pinyin:** hǎi
- **components:**
  - 氵(水)
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 每
    - měi
    - each

  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 每 (měi) ->
    - sea; ocean
  - **interpretation:** The character 海(hǎi, "sea; ocean") combines the semantic component 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water"), representing water or fluidity, with the phonetic component 每 (měi), which provides the pronunciation. The meaning of 'sea or ocean' naturally extends from the association with water, emphasizing a large body of it.
- **examples:**
  - 孩( )子( )们(們)喜( )欢(歡)去( )海( )边(邊)玩( )耍( )。

    - The blue of the ocean is refreshing.
  - 他( )梦(夢)想( )去( )环(環)游(遊)世( )界( )的( )海( )洋( )。
    - Tā mèngxiǎng qù huányóu shìjiè de hǎiyáng.

### 海派 → 海 → 每 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)后(後)，小( )屮( )冲(沖)破( )泥( )土( )而( )出( )。

### 海派 → 海 → 每 → 母
- **definition:** mother
- **pinyin:** mǔ
- **components:**
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** differentiated form
  - **description:**
    - 女 (nǚ, "woman") + addition of two dots ->
    - distinguished as 母 (mǔ, "mother")
  - **interpretation:** The character 母 (mǔ, "mother") is a differentiated form of 女 (nǚ, "woman") with the addition of two dots to distinguish it. In early script forms, both 母 (mǔ, "mother") and 女 (nǚ, "woman") were represented by the same form as 女, necessitating the addition of dots to create a visual distinction. The character 毋, originally borrowed from 母, further specialized by changing the dots to a stroke to avoid confusion between the characters.
- **examples:**
  - 母( )给(給)了( )我( )无(無)限( )的( )温(溫)暖( )。
    - mǔ gěi le wǒ wúxiàn de wēnnuǎn
    - Mother has given me endless warmth.
  - 我( )的( )母( )温(溫)柔( )而( )坚(堅)毅( )，培( )养(養)了( )我( )良( )好( )的( )品( )格( )。
    - wǒ de mǔ wēnróu ér jiānyì, péiyǎng le wǒ liánghǎo de pǐngé
    - My mother is gentle and strong, nurturing my good character.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 母](@media/glyph6bcd.png)
### 海派 → 海 → 每 → 母 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )位( )才( )华(華)横(橫)溢( )的( )女( )，赢(贏)得( )了( )全( )场(場)注( )目( )。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古( )时(時)候( )‘女( )’常( )被( )用( )来(來)象( )征(徵)温(溫)柔( )，而( )如( )今( )它( )代( )表( )独(獨)立( )自( )信( )。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

### 海派 → 派
- **definition:** style; group; faction; school
- **pinyin:** pài
- **components:**
  - 水
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 𠂢
    - mǐ
    - original form
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram: 𠂢 (original form) ->
    - Phono-semantic: semantic 水 (shuǐ, "water; river") + phonetic 𠂢 =
    - differentiation of original form with water
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted 𠂢 alone. To differentiate and specify meanings related to water or a flowing style, 水 (shuǐ, "water; river") was added as a semantic element.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)研( )究( )传(傳)统(統)文( )人( )派( )，注( )重( )文( )化( )底( )蕴(蘊)。

    - He joined the rock group to pursue a spirit of freedom.

    - Gǔdiǎn yīnyuè pài, jùyǒu yōujiǔ lìshǐ.

### 海派 → 派 → 水
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flowing water
  - **interpretation:** 水 (shuǐ, 'water') is a pictogram that directly represents the appearance of flowing water, making it intuitive and easy to recognize. Its simplicity and direct visual reference to its meaning have allowed it to remain unchanged over millennia.
- **examples:**
  - 水( )是( )一( )种(種)生( )命( )之( )源( )。
    - Shuǐ shì yī zhǒng shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 夏( )天( )很( )热(熱)，喝水能解暑。
    - Xiàtiān hěn rè, hē shuǐ néng jiě shǔ.
    - It is very hot in summer, drinking water can relieve the heat.
  - 河水潺潺，沿( )岸( )绿(綠)树(樹)成( )荫(蔭)。
    - Hé shuǐ chánchán, yán'àn lǜshù chéng yīn.
    - The river flows babbling, and green trees along the bank provide shade.

### 海派 → 派 → 𠂢
- **definition:** original form
- **pinyin:** mǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a long river with tributaries ->
    - original form
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠂢 is a pictographic representation of a long river with tributaries, symbolizing its original form as it visually attempts to capture the imagery of flowing water and branching paths. It is described as the horizontal flip of 永 (yǒng, meaning 'eternal'), though its depiction clearly relates more to an aquatic landscape than an everlasting concept.

## 点(點)茶( )
---
## traditional tea whisking method
### diǎn chá
---
- **traditional:** 點茶
- **definition:** traditional tea whisking method
- **pinyin:** diǎn chá
- **components:**
  - 点(點)
    - diǎn
    - point; dot; order
  - 茶
    - chá
    - tea
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 點 (diǎn, "point; dot; order") + 茶 (chá, "tea")
  - **interpretation:** 點 (diǎn, "point; dot; order") originally refers to making a small mark or selecting. In the context of 點茶 (diǎn chá), it refers to the action of whisking or preparing tea, traditionally involving adding water drop by drop while whisking the tea into a frothy mixture. This process mirrors the careful, precise act of 点 (diǎn, "point; dot") where tea is methodically introduced and transformed. 茶 (chá, "tea") brings in the context of the beverage itself, emphasizing the ritualistic and artisanal process involved.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )喜( )欢(歡)研( )究( )点(點)茶( )的( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Tā xǐhuān yánjiū diǎn chá de lìshǐ.
    - He likes to study the history of traditional tea whisking.
  - 在( )宋( )代( )，点(點)茶( )是( )一( )种(種)流( )行( )的( )艺(藝)术(術)形( )式( )。
    - Zài Sòng dài, diǎn chá shì yī zhǒng liúxíng de yìshù xíngshì.
    - During the Song Dynasty, tea whisking was a popular art form.
  - 茶( )艺(藝)师(師)展( )示( )了( )点(點)茶( )的( )技( )巧( )。
    - Cháyìshī zhǎnshìle diǎn chá de jìqiǎo.
    - The tea artist demonstrated the technique of traditional tea whisking.
### 点(點)茶( ) → 点(點)
- **traditional:** 點
- **definition:** point; dot; order
- **pinyin:** diǎn
- **components:**
  - 黑
    - hēi
    - black
  - 占
    - zhān
    - divination
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 黑 (hēi, "black") + phonetic: 占 (zhān, "divination") =
    - black mark indicating a point ->
    - spot, dot
  - **interpretation:** In 點 (diǎn, "dot"), 黑 (hēi, "black") represents the concept of a mark or dot in its dark color, while 占 (zhān, "divination") provides the phonetic spelling. Together, the components denote a small dark mark or point.
  - **simplification:** 点(點) simplifies 點 by removing the upper components of 黑 (hēi, "black"), forming a more straightforward symbol for a dot or small point.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)在( )图(圖)上( )点(點)出( )目( )标(標)。
    - Qǐng zài tú shàng diǎn chū mùbiāo。
    - Please mark the target on the map.
  - 她( )用( )粉( )笔(筆)在( )黑( )板( )上( )点(點)了( )点(點)，指明答案。
    - Tā yòng fěnbǐ zài hēibǎn shàng diǎn le diǎn, zhǐmíng dá'àn。
    - She lightly tapped on the blackboard with chalk to indicate the answer.
  - 网(網)格( )中( )的( )每( )个(個)点(點)都( )很( )重( )要( )。
    - Wǎnggé zhōng de měi gè diǎn dōu hěn zhòngyào。
    - Every point in the grid is important.
### 点(點)茶( ) → 点(點) → 黑
- **definition:** black
- **pinyin:** hēi
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - person
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 大 (dà, "person") with a tattooed face for penal purposes ->
    - ancient punishments ->
    - dots added around 大 representing tattoo marks ->
    - erroneously interpreted as 火 (huǒ, "fire") under a chimney causing blackening ->
    - displaced 玄 (xuán, "black")
  - **interpretation:** The character 黑(hēi) originally represented a person with facial tattoos, symbolizing punishment. Over time, its meaning evolved to represent the color black, replacing 玄 (xuán, "black") which was previously used.
  - **simplification:** The character is not simplified in Chinese. However, in Japanese, the modern form 黒 replaces two dots with one stroke as part of orthographic reform.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)只( )乌(烏)鸦(鴉)的( )羽( )毛( )非( )常( )黑( )。
    - Zhè zhī wūyā de yǔmáo fēicháng hēi.
    - The crow's feathers are very black.
  - 他( )的( )心( )情( )因( )为(為)失( )落( )而( )变(變)得( )黑( )，看( )不( )出( )一( )丝(絲)笑( )容( )。
    - Tā de xīnqíng yīnwèi shīluò ér biànde hēi, kànbùchū yīsī xiàoróng.
    - His mood turned dark because of the loss, showing no trace of a smile.
  - 黑( )色( )在( )时(時)尚( )中( )代( )表( )神( )秘( )。
    - Hēisè zài shíshàng zhōng dàibiǎo shénmì.
    - Black represents mystery in fashion.

### 点(點)茶( ) → 点(點) → 黑 → 大
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房( )子( )很( )大( )。
    - Zhè ge fángzi hěn dà.
    - This house is very big.

  - 大( )人( )物( )登( )场(場)，留( )下( )传(傳)奇( )。
    - Dà rénwù dēngchǎng, liúxià chuánqí.

### 点(點)茶( ) → 点(點) → 黑 → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.
- **examples:**
  - 此( )夫( )心( )怀(懷)大( )志( )。
    - Cǐ fū xīn huái dà zhì.
    - This man has lofty aspirations.
  - 他( )勤( )劳(勞)努( )力( )，堪( )称(稱)良( )夫( )。
    - Tā qín láo nǔ lì, kān chēng liáng fū.
    - He works diligently and is regarded as an exemplary man.

### 点(點)茶( ) → 点(點) → 占 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.

    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.

### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶
- **definition:** tea
- **pinyin:** chá
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 余
    - yú
    - I; surplus
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") + phonetic 余 (yú) ->
    - modified from archaic 荼 (bitter plant) for tea
  - **interpretation:** The character 茶 (chá, "tea") combines 艹 (cǎo, "grass") as the semantic element, indicating a plant-related concept, with 余 (yú) serving as the phonetic component. Originally, 茶 was a modification of the archaic character 荼 which referred to a 'bitter plant.' This association with a bitter plant reflects the historical use of tea leaves, which have a bitter taste, thereby making 茶 appropriate for representing 'tea.'
- **examples:**
  - 奶奶每天早上喝茶。
    - Nǎinai měitiān zǎoshang hē chá.
    - Grandma drinks tea every morning.
  - 这(這)家( )茶( )馆(館)的( )绿(綠)茶( )味( )道( )很( )好( )。
    - Zhè jiā cháguǎn de lǜchá wèidào hěn hǎo.
    - The green tea at this teahouse tastes very good.
  - 你( )想( )喝( )红(紅)茶( )还(還)是( )绿(綠)茶( )？
    - Nǐ xiǎng hē hóngchá háishì lǜchá?
    - Do you want to drink black tea or green tea?
### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )写(寫)字( )时(時)用( )艹( )作( )草( )字( )的( )偏( )旁( )。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春( )天( )到( )来(來)时(時)，艹( )生( )长(長)得( )很( )快( )。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.
### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘)
- **traditional:** 餘
- **definition:** I; surplus
- **pinyin:** yú
- **components:**
  - 食
    - shí
    - food
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 食 (shí, 'food') + phonetic 余(餘) (yú, 'I') ->
    - remains of food ->
    - 'excess, surplus'
  - **interpretation:** The character 餘 evolved to represent the concept of 'excess' or 'surplus' through a phono-semantic compound. It combines the semantic component 食 (shí, 'food'), representing food or consumption, with the phonetic component 余(餘) (yú, 'I'), to indicate leftovers or remains of food. This directly suggests an aspect of having more than what is needed, thus an 'excess' or 'surplus'.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 餘 was simplified to 余 by removing the semantic component 食 (shí, 'food'), leaving only the phonetic component.
- **examples:**
  - 余(餘)愿(願)以( )诗(詩)书(書)为(為)乐(樂)。
    - Yú yuàn yǐ shīshū wéi lè.
    - I wish to take pleasure in poetry and books.
  - 余(餘)在此地，心( )安( )吾( )归(歸)。
    - Yú zài cǐdì, xīn ān wú guī.
    - I am here, at peace and at home.
  - 余(餘)莫( )负(負)此( )生( )。
    - Yú mò fù cǐ shēng.
    - I should not waste this life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 余](@media/glyph4f59.png)
### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘) → 食
- **definition:** food
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - assemble
  - 𠊊
    - jí
    - bowl with stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:** 亼 (jí, "assemble") over a pictographic bowl of rice on a stand, symbolized by 𠊊 (jí, "bowl with stand")
  - **interpretation:** Initially, the character 食 (shí, "eat") visually represented a mouth over a bowl of rice, conveying the act of eating or a meal intuitively through this imagery.
- **examples:**
  - 他食得很快。
    - Tā shí dé hěn kuài.
    - He eats very quickly.
  - 我( )准(準)备(備)午( )食( )，与(與)朋( )友( )共( )享( )佳( )肴(餚)。
    - Wǒ zhǔnbèi wǔ shí, yǔ péngyǒu gòngxiǎng jiāyáo.
    - I am preparing lunch to share a delicious meal with my friends.
  - 民( )以( )食( )为(為)天( )。
    - Mín yǐ shí wéi tiān.
    - Food is regarded as the most important element for the people.
### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘) → 食 → 亼
- **definition:** assemble
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)
### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘) → 食 → 亼 → 入
- **definition:** enter
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入( )座( )。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生( )走( )入( )校( )园(園)，开(開)始( )新( )学(學)期( )。
    - Xuéshēng zǒu rù xiàoyuán, kāishǐ xīn xuéqī.
    - The students enter the campus and start a new semester.
  - 游(遊)客( )走( )入( )古( )城( )，探( )索( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Yóukè zǒu rù gǔchéng, tànsuǒ lìshǐ.
    - The tourists enter the ancient city and explore its history.

### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘) → 食 → 亼 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他( )只( )看( )到( )一( )只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了( )花( )园(園)。

  - 一( )条(條)直( )路( )通( )向( )远(遠)方( )。

### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘) → 食 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)不( )错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在( )是( )吃( )晚( )饭(飯)的( )时(時)候( )。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她( )今( )天( )特( )别(別)忙( )，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面( )。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘) → 食 → 𠊊
- **definition:** bowl with stand
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - mouth
  - 皀
    - jí
    - bowl of rice on a stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 亼 (mouth) over 皀 (bowl of rice on a stand) ->
    - depicts a bowl with a stand
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠊊 visually represents a mouth above a bowl of rice on a stand, indicating a utensil or vessel used for holding food. This image directly links to the idea of a 'bowl with stand.' The component 皀 specifically conveys the idea of a container or bowl elevated, which situates its primary meaning in the context of serving or holding food.
### 点(點)茶( ) → 茶 → 余(餘) → 食 → 𠊊 → 皀

    - part of the radical 食 (shí, "food")
  - **interpretation:** The character 皀(bá, "acorn") depicts a bowl of rice on a stand, aligning it with food-related imagery.

## 串串香
---
## skewered hot pot
### chuàn chuàn xiāng
---
- **definition:** skewered hot pot
- **pinyin:** chuàn chuàn xiāng
- **components:**
  - 串串
    - chuànchuàn
    - a series of skewers
  - 香
    - xiāng
    - fragrant; aromatic; savory
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** In this word, 串 (chuàn, "skewer") is the main concept of skewering food; repeated to 串串 (chuànchuàn, "a series of skewers"), and 香 (xiāng, "fragrant") refers to the aroma from cooking or seasoning, describing the aromatic quality of the dish.
  - **interpretation:** 串串 (chuànchuàn, "a series of skewers") signifies multiple skewered items, a defining characteristic of this dining style where small portions are cooked on skewers. 香 (xiāng, "fragrant") emphasizes the appealing scent released as the ingredients cook in the hot pot broth, drawing people in with its aroma. This describes a type of hot pot where individual skewers of ingredients are cooked in a communal pot, appealing both visually and aromatically.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)昨( )天( )晚( )上( )去( )吃( )了( )串( )串( )香( )。
    - Wǒmen zuótiān wǎnshàng qù chī le chuàn chuàn xiāng.
    - We went to eat skewered hot pot last night.
  - 小( )李( )特( )别(別)喜( )欢(歡)成( )都( )的( )串( )串( )香( )。
    - Xiǎo Lǐ tèbié xǐhuān Chéngdū de chuàn chuàn xiāng.
    - Xiao Li especially likes Chengdu's skewered hot pot.
  - 串( )串( )香( )的( )汤(湯)底( )有( )很( )多( )种(種)口( )味( )，可( )以( )根( )据(據)自( )己( )的( )喜( )好( )选(選)择(擇)。
    - Chuàn chuàn xiāng de tāngdǐ yǒu hěn duō zhǒng kǒuwèi, kěyǐ gēnjù zìjǐ de xǐhào xuǎnzé.
    - The skewered hot pot has many flavors of broth to choose from according to your preference.
### 串串香 → 串串
- **definition:** a series of skewers
- **pinyin:** chuànchuàn
- **components:**
  - 串
    - chuàn
    - string together; skewer
  - 串
    - chuàn
    - string together; skewer
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 串 (chuàn, "string together") + 串 (chuàn, "string together") refers to food items pierced and cooked on skewers.
  - **interpretation:** The repetition of 串 (chuàn, "string together") emphasizes the act of threading ingredients onto a skewer, which is common in street food culture where various meats and vegetables are skewered together and grilled.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)吃( )串( )串( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī chuànchuàn.
    - I like eating skewered food.
  - 冬( )天( )寒( )冷( )时(時)，串( )串( )让(讓)人( )感( )觉(覺)温(溫)暖( )。
    - Dōngtiān hánlěng shí, chuànchuàn ràng rén gǎnjué wēnnuǎn.
    - When winter is cold, skewers make people feel warm.
  - 夜( )市( )里(裡)，各( )种(種)美( )味( )的( )串( )串( )吸( )引( )顾(顧)客( )。
    - Yèshì lǐ, gèzhǒng měiwèi de chuànchuàn xīyǐn gùkè.
    - In the night market, various delicious skewers attract customers.
### 串串香 → 串串 → 串
- **definition:** string together; skewer
- **pinyin:** chuàn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts objects strung together
  - **interpretation:** The character 串(chuàn) visually represents the concept of objects strung together, often like beads or skewers. This straightforward pictographic representation effectively conveys its meaning as 'to string together' or 'skewer'.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )铁(鐵)签(簽)串( )起( )葡( )萄( )，准(準)备(備)烧(燒)烤( )。
    - Tā yòng tiě qiān chuàn qǐ pútao, zhǔnbèi shāokǎo.
    - He skewered the grapes with an iron skewer, preparing for a barbecue.
  - 她( )把( )各( )色( )小( )灯(燈)笼(籠)串( )成( )一( )条(條)彩( )带(帶)，装(裝)点(點)夜( )宵( )。
    - Tā bǎ gèsè xiǎo dēnglóng chuàn chéng yī tiáo cǎidài, zhuāngdiǎn yèxiāo.
    - She strung various small lanterns together into a colorful ribbon, decorating the night market.
  - 老( )板( )让(讓)工( )人( )把( )散( )乱(亂)的( )零( )件( )串( )起( )来(來)，以( )便( )机(機)器( )组(組)装(裝)。
    - Lǎobǎn ràng gōngrén bǎ sǎnluàn de língjiàn chuàn qǐlái, yǐbiàn jīqì zǔzhuāng.
    - The boss had the workers string together the scattered parts, so that the machine could be assembled.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 串](@media/glyph4e32.png)
### 串串香 → 香
- **definition:** fragrant; aromatic; savory
- **pinyin:** xiāng
- **components:**
  - 黍
    - shǔ
    - glutinous millet
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 甘
    - gān
    - sweet
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - say
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 黍 (shǔ, "glutinous millet") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") ->
    - millet used for liquor ->
    - 甘 (gān, "sweet") replaced 口, indicating sweetness ->
    - 禾 + 曰 final form
  - **interpretation:** The character 香(xiāng) originated from showcasing millet as a beverage ingredient, hinting at the fragrant nature of such products. Over time, the components evolved to stress the sweet and fragrant aspect, becoming 禾 and 曰 to convey aroma.
- **examples:**
  - 花( )儿(兒)散( )发(發)出( )香( )气(氣)。
    - Huār sànfā chū xiāngqì.
    - The flowers emit a fragrant scent.
  - 这(這)汤(湯)闻(聞)起( )来(來)很( )香( )。
    - Zhè tāng wén qǐlái hěn xiāng.
    - This soup smells very fragrant.
  - 她的香水味迷人，让(讓)人( )陶( )醉( )。
    - Tā de xiāngshuǐ wèi mírén, ràng rén táozuì.
    - Her perfume is enchanting, making people intoxicated.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 香](@media/glyph9999.png)
### 串串香 → 香 → 黍
- **definition:** glutinous millet
- **pinyin:** shǔ
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - cereal
  - 水
    - shuǐ
    - water
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts 禾 (hé, "cereal") with 水 (shuǐ, "water") under it ->
    - symbolizing millet with wine or its sticky nature
  - **interpretation:** The character 黍 (shǔ, "glutinous millet") visually combines the image of a cereal plant with droplets or signs of water beneath it, likely indicating the wine made from millet or its water-resistant qualities. Alternatively, it highlights millet's unique growing conditions.
- **examples:**
  - 秋( )天( )时(時)，农(農)夫( )收( )获(穫)黍( )。
    - Qiūtiān shí, nóngfū shōuhuò shǔ.
    - In autumn, the farmer harvests glutinous millet.
  - 古人以黍，寓( )意( )丰(豐)收( )。
    - Gǔrén yǐ shǔ, yùyì fēngshōu.
    - The ancients used glutinous millet to symbolize a bountiful harvest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 黍](@media/glyph9ecd.png)
### 串串香 → 香 → 黍 → 禾
- **definition:** cereal
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收( )获(穫)的( )禾( )香( )弥(彌)漫( )在( )田( )野( )中( )。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民( )辛( )勤( )耕( )作( )，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)了( )禾( )苗( )，预(預)示( )着(著)丰(豐)收( )。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.

### 串串香 → 香 → 黍 → 水

- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flowing water
  - **interpretation:** 水 (shuǐ, 'water') is a pictogram that directly represents the appearance of flowing water, making it intuitive and easy to recognize. Its simplicity and direct visual reference to its meaning have allowed it to remain unchanged over millennia.
- **examples:**
  - 水( )是( )一( )种(種)生( )命( )之( )源( )。

    - Xiàtiān hěn rè, hē shuǐ néng jiě shǔ.
    - It is very hot in summer, drinking water can relieve the heat.
  - 河水潺潺，沿( )岸( )绿(綠)树(樹)成( )荫(蔭)。
    - Hé shuǐ chánchán, yán'àn lǜshù chéng yīn.

### 串串香 → 香 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

### 串串香 → 香 → 甘

  - **description:**
    - 𠁿 ->

  - **interpretation:** 甘 (gān, "sweet") is an ideogram depicting something sweet inside an open mouth. This visualization of taste illustrates the core concept of sweetness as directly related to the act of consuming something pleasant. This visual representation connects the sensory experience of sweetness with its meaning in the character.

  - 这(這)种(種)水( )果( )味( )道( )甘( )美( )。

### 串串香 → 香 → 曰

  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老( )师(師)曰( )：勤( )奋(奮)是( )成( )功( )之( )母( )。

## 秋葵
---
## okra
### qiū kuí
---
- **definition:** okra
- **pinyin:** qiū kuí
- **components:**
  - 秋
    - qiū
    - autumn
  - 葵
    - kuí
    - mallow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 秋 (qiū, "autumn") 葵 (kuí, "mallow")
  - **interpretation:** The character 秋 (qiū, "autumn") reflects the harvest season, associated with crops reaching maturity, and identifies the time for harvesting many vegetables. 葵 (kuí, "mallow") represents okra as it belongs to the mallow family. Thus, 秋葵 (qiū kuí) describes okra as a plant that matures and is harvested around autumn, belonging to the mallow family.
- **examples:**
  - 秋葵是( )绿(綠)色( )的( )蔬( )菜( )。
    - Qiūkuí shì lǜsè de shūcài.
    - Okra is a green vegetable.
  - 我( )最( )喜( )欢(歡)炒( )秋( )葵( )。
    - Wǒ zuì xǐhuān chǎo qiūkuí.

### 秋葵 → 秋
- **definition:** autumn
- **pinyin:** qiū
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 禾 (hé, 'grain') + 火 (huǒ, 'fire') =
    - grain + fire ->
    - harvest time ->
    - autumn
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 'grain' and 'fire', symbolizing the practice of burning fields after harvest, marking autumn as harvest time.
- **examples:**
  - 秋( )天( )来(來)了( )。
    - Qiū tiān lái le.
    - Autumn has arrived.
  - 秋( )风(風)送( )爽( )，稻( )谷(穀)金( )黄(黃)。

    - The autumn breeze brings coolness, and the rice is golden.

    - Zài qiū jì de wǔ hòu, shū xiāng mǎn shì.

  - **interpretation:** The character 葵 combines the semantic component 艹, indicating 'grass' or 'plant', with the phonetic component 癸, which provides the sound. This structure denotes a kind of plant, which can include mallow, sunflower, or hibiscus based on context.

### 秋葵 → 葵 → 癸
- **definition:** tenth heavenly stem
- **pinyin:** guǐ
- **components:**
  - 戣
    - kuí
    - halberd
  - 葵
    - kuí
    - mallow
  - 規
    - guī

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 癸 depicts a form whose original meaning is uncertain ->
    - associated with measuring tools or setups for determining directions and solstices ->
    - possible original forms of 戣 (kuí, "halberd"), 葵 (kuí, "mallow"), 規 (guī, "compass; rule")
  - **interpretation:** The character 癸 (guǐ, "tenth earthly branch") is a pictogram whose depiction is uncertain but is conceptually linked to measurement or orientation tools. These tools were possibly used for solar observations or direction finding, thus lending the character significance in calendrical or positional contexts.
- **examples:**

### 秋葵 → 葵 → 癸 → 戣 → 魏 → 委

- **pinyin:** wěi
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**

  - **description:**
    - phonetic 禾 (hé, "grain") + semantic 女 (nǚ, "woman") ->
    - entrust
  - **interpretation:** The character 委 combines 禾 (hé, "grain") as the phonetic component to suggest sound, with 女 (nǚ, "woman") as the semantic component. Originally, the oracle bone representation used 𠃊, depicting a figure kneeling, which aligns with the idea of yielding or resigning. Hence, the combination implies entrusting or assigning a task, as one might with a trusted companion or subordinate.
- **examples:**

### 秋葵 → 葵 → 癸 → 戣 → 魏 → 鬼

  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling man or figure with an ugly face (甶) + small 厶 (trace of tail) added later
  - **interpretation:** The character 鬼 (guǐ, "demon") visually represents a kneeling figure with a distinctive, mask-like face, evoking the image of a supernatural being or ghost. The addition of a small 厶 suggests a residual tail, enhancing its demon-like appearance. This depiction highlights the character's association with eerie, otherworldly entities.

### 秋葵 → 葵 → 癸 → 規
- **definition:** compass; rule
- **pinyin:** guī
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - husband
  - 癸
    - guǐ
    - tenth heavenly stem
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram of a compass ->
    - transformed to combine 夫 (fū, "husband") + a phonetic component similar to 癸
  - **interpretation:** The character 規 (guī, "compass") originally depicted a cross-shaped measuring compass. Over time, it evolved to incorporate elements for phonetic reasons—specifically, adopting an abbreviated form of the phonetic component 癸 (guǐ, "tenth heavenly stem"). The association with 夫 (fū, "husband") originally related to the tool-like function of a compass in measurement.
  - **simplification:** 规(規): 見 component was removed and replaced with 见, a simpler form, preserving the phonetic similarity.
- **examples:**
  - 老( )师(師)教( )我( )们(們)如( )何( )使( )用( )规(規)。
    - Lǎoshī jiāo wǒmen rúhé shǐyòng guī.
    - The teacher teaches us how to use a compass.
  - 建( )筑(築)师(師)利( )用( )规(規)和( )尺( )来(來)绘(繪)制(製)蓝(藍)图(圖)。
    - Jiànzhùshī lìyòng guī hé chǐ lái huìzhì lántú.
    - The architect uses a compass and ruler to draft blueprints.
  - 古( )代( )的( )工( )匠( )依( )靠( )简(簡)单(單)的( )规(規)和( )工( )具( )制(製)作( )精( )美( )的( )器( )物( )。
    - Gǔdài de gōngjiàng yīkào jiǎndān de guī hé gōngjù zhìzuò jīngměi de qìwù.
    - Ancient artisans relied on simple compasses and tools to craft exquisite artifacts.

### 秋葵 → 葵 → 癸 → 規 → 夫

### 秋葵 → 葵 → 癸 → 規 → 夫 → 大
- **definition:** big
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**

  - 大( )人( )物( )登( )场(場)，留( )下( )传(傳)奇( )。

## 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( )
---
## pink rose
### fěn hóng méi guī
---
- **traditional:** 粉紅玫瑰
- **definition:** pink rose
- **pinyin:** fěn hóng méi guī
- **components:**
  - 粉紅
    - fěnhóng
    - pink
  - 玫瑰
    - méiguī
    - rose
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 粉 (fěn, "powder; pink") and 紅 (hóng, "red") together form 粉紅 (fěnhóng, "pink"), indicating the light shade of red. 玫瑰 (méiguī, "rose") refers to the flower.
  - **interpretation:** The term 粉紅 (fěnhóng, "pink") combines 粉 (fěn, "powder") to imply a softer, lighter version of 紅 (hóng, "red"), creating the pastel color pink. 玫瑰 (méiguī, "rose") refers to the flower known for its association with romance and beauty. Together, 粉紅玫瑰 (fěnhóng méiguī, "pink rose") evokes the image of a rose colored in a gentle shade of pink.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )收( )到( )了( )很( )多( )粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( )。
    - Tā shōu dào le hěn duō fěn hóng méi guī.
    - She received many pink roses.
  - 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( )的( )香( )味( )令人陶醉。
    - Fěn hóng méi guī de xiāngwèi lìng rén táozuì.
    - The fragrance of pink roses is intoxicating.
  - 在( )花( )园(園)里(裡)，粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( )盛( )开(開)的( )时(時)候( )，令( )人( )感( )到( )无(無)比( )幸( )福( )。
    - Zài huāyuán lǐ, fěn hóng méi guī shèngkāi de shíhòu, lìng rén gǎndào wúbǐ xìngfú.
    - In the garden, when the pink roses are in full bloom, it brings incomparable happiness.
### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 粉紅
- **definition:** pink
- **pinyin:** fěnhóng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 粉 (fěn, "powder") + 紅 (hóng, "red") =
    - powdery red ->
    - pink
  - **interpretation:** The term 粉紅(fěnhóng) derives its meaning from combining 粉 (fěn, "powder"), which evokes a sense of lightness and dilution, with 紅 (hóng, "red"), which provides the base color. The combination suggests a red that has been lightened or softened into a pink hue, akin to the appearance of red when mixed with white powder.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)粉( )红(紅)色( )的( )花( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān fěnhóng sè de huā.
    - I like pink flowers.
  - 她( )穿( )了( )一( )件( )粉( )红(紅)裙( )子( )。
    - Tā chuānle yī jiàn fěnhóng qúnzi.
    - She wore a pink dress.
  - 这(這)面( )墙(牆)是( )粉( )红(紅)色( )的( )，感( )觉(覺)很( )温(溫)暖( )。
    - Zhè miàn qiáng shì fěnhóng sè de, gǎnjué hěn wēnnuǎn.
    - This wall is pink, and it feels very warm.
### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 粉紅 → 紅
- **definition:** red; popular; revolution; bonus
- **pinyin:** hóng
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk
  - 工
    - gōng
    - work
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 糸 (mì, "silk") + phonetic 工 (gōng) ->
    - red
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 糸 (mì, "silk"), illustrating the context of dyed or colored silk, with the phonetic 工 (gōng), offering the pronunciation. The use of silk relates to the traditional skill of dyeing fabric, specifically producing the color red.
  - **simplification:** Simplified as 红, where 糸 (mì, "silk") was replaced by the simplified radical 纟, reducing strokes while keeping the character's meaning intact.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )脸(臉)红(紅)了( )。

    - His face turned red.

### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 玫瑰
- **definition:** rose
- **pinyin:** méiguī
- **components:**
  - 玫
    - méi
    - rose gemstone; beautiful small stone
  - 瑰
    - guī
    - rare; precious; exceptional
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 玫 (méi, "rose gemstone; beautiful small stone") has a historical association with something small, precious, and beautiful, similar to a gemstone. 瑰 (guī, "rare; precious; exceptional") emphasizes uniqueness and value, often referring to something remarkable or extraordinary. Together, 玫瑰 (méiguī, "rose") evokes the image of a precious and exceptionally beautiful flower.
  - **interpretation:** 玫 (méi, "rose gemstone; beautiful small stone") focuses on beauty and preciousness, suggesting something delicate and charming like a gemstone. 瑰 (guī, "rare; precious; exceptional") highlights the unique and extraordinary qualities of the rose, marking it as a rare flower of great beauty. The combination implies an exquisite, highly valued flower—like a 'gem among flowers', hence the concept of a rose.
- **examples:**
  - 玫( )瑰( )花( )开(開)得( )很( )美( )。
    - Méi guī huā kāi de hěn měi.
    - The rose blooms beautifully.
  - 她( )收( )到( )了( )一( )束( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( )。
    - Tā shōu dào le yī shù hóng méi guī.
    - She received a bouquet of red roses.
  - 玫( )瑰( )象( )征(徵)爱(愛)情( )。
    - Méi guī xiàng zhēng ài qíng.
    - Roses symbolize love.
### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 玫瑰 → 玫
- **definition:** rose gemstone; beautiful small stone
- **pinyin:** méi
- **components:**
  - 𤣩
    - (jade
    - a type of jade
  - 文
    - wén
    - script; pattern
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** semantic 𤣩 (jade) + phonetic 文 (sound)
  - **interpretation:** 玫 (méi) combines the semantic 𤣩, meaning "jade," with the phonetic component 文 (wén) to convey the sound. The character is used to denote a type of jade, leveraging 𤣩 to evoke the preciousness and craftsmanship associated with jade.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )戴( )了( )一( )串( )玫( )玉( )项(項)链(鏈)。
    - Tā dài le yī chuàn méi yù xiàngliàn.
    - She wore a necklace with rose jade.
  - 玫( )石( )被( )雕( )刻( )成( )精( )美( )的( )饰(飾)品( )。
    - Méi shí bèi diāokè chéng jīngměi de shìpǐn.
    - The rose jade was carved into exquisite ornaments.
  - 这(這)种(種)玫( )石( )在( )市( )场(場)上( )非( )常( )受( )欢(歡)迎( )。
    - Zhè zhǒng méi shí zài shìchǎng shàng fēicháng shòu huānyíng.
    - This type of rose jade is very popular in the market.
### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 玫瑰 → 玫 → 𤣩
- **definition:** a type of jade
- **pinyin:** (jade
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a cong (ritual jade totem)
  - **interpretation:** The character 𤣩 is a variant form of 玉 (yù, "jade"), which originally depicted a cong, a type of ritual jade totem. Over time, a dot was added to distinguish it from 王 (wáng, "king") due to the visual similarity between the two characters. Jade played a significant role in art and rituals, which is why its pictogram was distinctly designed. The character represents the material jade and its cultural significance as a precious and spiritual object.
### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 玫瑰 → 玫 → 文
- **definition:** script; pattern
- **pinyin:** wén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crested animal pattern, representing patterns of writing.
  - **interpretation:** 文 (wén, 'language; culture') originally depicted a symbol or pattern on objects, which is closely related to text and writing as forms of patterned representation, embodying cultural expression.
- **examples:**
  - 他研究古文。
    - Tā yánjiū gǔwén.
    - He studies classical literature.
  - 我( )们(們)的( )文( )化( )深( )厚( )，文( )学(學)绵(綿)长(長)悠( )远(遠)。
    - Wǒmen de wénhuà shēnhòu, wénxué miáncháng yōuyuǎn.
    - Our culture is profound, and our literature is long and far-reaching.
  - 书(書)中( )蕴(蘊)含( )丰(豐)厚( )的( )文( )采( )。
    - Shū zhōng yùnhán fēnghòu de wéncǎi.
    - The book is imbued with rich literary elegance.

### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 玫瑰 → 瑰

- **pinyin:** guī
- **components:**
  - 𤣩
    - yù
    - jade
  - 鬼
    - guǐ
    - ghost
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 𤣩 (jade) + phonetic 鬼 ->
    - extraordinary; precious
  - **interpretation:** 瑰 uses 𤣩 (jade) to signify something valuable and beautiful, with 鬼 contributing the sound. Jade, being a precious stone, naturally leads to the meaning 'precious.' The phonetic 鬼 does not contribute meaning here but provides the pronunciation, guiding the sense of 'extraordinary' as being distinct or remarkable, much like the unique and distinguished nature of precious jade.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)些( )宝(寶)石( )看( )起( )来(來)非( )常( )瑰( )丽(麗)。

### 粉( )红(紅)玫( )瑰( ) → 玫瑰 → 瑰 → 鬼
- **definition:** ghost
- **pinyin:** guǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling man or figure with an ugly face (甶) + small 厶 (trace of tail) added later
  - **interpretation:** The character 鬼 (guǐ, "demon") visually represents a kneeling figure with a distinctive, mask-like face, evoking the image of a supernatural being or ghost. The addition of a small 厶 suggests a residual tail, enhancing its demon-like appearance. This depiction highlights the character's association with eerie, otherworldly entities.
- **examples:**
  - 深( )夜( )独(獨)行( )时(時)，忽( )遇( )鬼( )影( )飘(飄)忽( )。

## 粽子
---
## rice dumpling
### zòng zi
---
- **definition:** rice dumpling
- **pinyin:** zòng zi
- **components:**
  - 粽
    - zòng
    - sticky rice wrapped in bamboo leaves
  - 子
    - zi
    - child; small thing
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 粽 (zòng, "sticky rice wrapped in bamboo leaves"), 子 (zi, "child; small thing")
  - **interpretation:** 粽 (zòng, "sticky rice wrapped in bamboo leaves") refers directly to the traditional food item of sticky rice cooked in leaves. 子 (zi, "child; small thing") is often used in Chinese to denote a small or compact version of an object, essentially referring to a 'dumpling' or small parcel of food. Putting these together, 粽子 refers to the dish known as a rice dumpling, small packages of sticky rice encased in leaves, especially popular during the Dragon Boat Festival.
- **examples:**
  - 端( )午( )节(節)的( )时(時)候( )，我( )们(們)吃( )粽( )子( )。
    - Duānwǔ jié de shíhòu, wǒmen chī zòngzi.
    - During the Dragon Boat Festival, we eat rice dumplings.
  - 她( )亲(親)手( )包( )了( )很( )多( )粽( )子( )。
    - Tā qīnshǒu bāo le hěn duō zòngzi.
    - She made many rice dumplings by hand.
  - 粽子有甜的，也( )有( )咸(鹹)的( )。
    - Zòngzi yǒu tián de, yě yǒu xián de.
    - Rice dumplings can be sweet or savory.
### 粽子 → 粽(糉)
- **traditional:** 糉
- **definition:** sticky rice wrapped in bamboo leaves
- **pinyin:** zòng
- **components:**
  - 米
    - mǐ
    - rice
  - 㚇
    - zōng
    - carefree, easygoing
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 米 (mǐ, "rice") + phonetic 㚇 (zōng) ->
    - sticky rice wrapped in leaves
  - **interpretation:** The character 糉 originated as a phono-semantic compound where 米 (mǐ, "rice") indicates the semantic field relevant to rice, and 㚇 (zōng) provides the sound. Together they denote sticky rice wrapped in leaves, commonly referred to as 粽子 (zòngzi) in modern usage.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )端( )午( )节(節)吃( )粽(糉)子( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān zài duānwǔjié chī zòngzi.
    - I like to eat sticky rice wrapped in leaves during the Dragon Boat Festival.
  - 她( )在( )市( )场(場)上( )买(買)了( )很( )多( )粽(糉)子( )。
    - Tā zài shìchǎng shàng mǎile hěn duō zòngzi.
    - She bought a lot of sticky rice wrapped in leaves at the market.
  - 粽(糉)子( )的( )味( )道( )让(讓)我( )想( )起( )了( )童( )年( )。
    - Zòngzi de wèidào ràng wǒ xiǎngqǐle tóngnián.
    - The taste of sticky rice wrapped in leaves reminds me of my childhood.
### 粽子 → 粽(糉) → 米
- **definition:** rice
- **pinyin:** mǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts rice kernels ->
    - 米(mǐ, 'rice')
  - **interpretation:** The character 米(mǐ, 'rice') visually represents dehusked rice kernels to differentiate it from 粟. The horizontal stroke may symbolize a bamboo sieve, emphasizing the process of separating grains from their husks.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)吃( )米( )饭(飯)。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī mǐfàn.
    - I like to eat rice.
  - 她( )从(從)农(農)村( )带(帶)回( )一( )袋( )米( )，用( )来(來)煮( )饭(飯)。
    - Tā cóng nóngcūn dài huí yī dài mǐ, yòng lái zhǔ fàn.
    - She brought a bag of rice from the countryside to cook.
  - 市( )场(場)上( )有( )新( )米( )出( )售( )。
    - Shìchǎng shàng yǒu xīn mǐ chūshòu.
    - New rice is available in the market.

### 粽子 → 粽(糉) → 㚇 → 乑
- **definition:** together
- **pinyin:** yín
- **components:**
  - 眾
    - zhòng
    - multitude
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a sun (日) above three humans (㐺) ->
    - sun modified to resemble a horizontal eye (early form of 目) ->
    - a crowd under someone’s gaze ->
    - final form resembles 罒.
  - **interpretation:** The character 乑 is derived from 眾(众) (zhòng, "multitude"), symbolizing a crowd gathered under the gaze of the sun, reinterpreted as the eye of authority overseeing a collective group, representing the concept of 'together' or 'gathered'.
### 粽子 → 粽(糉) → 㚇 → 乑 → 眾
- **definition:** multitude
- **pinyin:** zhòng
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 日(日, "sun") above three 人(人, "person") ->
    - sun over a crowd ->
    - modified to 罒(resembles "eye") + three 人(人, "person") ->
    - crowd under gaze
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted the sun shining over three figures, indicating people gathered or working outdoors. This was modified over time with the top element stylized to resemble an eye watching over a crowd, symbolizing a multitude under observation.
- **examples:**
  - 人( )群( )聚( )集( )在( )广(廣)场(場)上( )，引( )起( )了( )围(圍)观(觀)者( )的( )注( )意( )。
    - Rénqún jùjí zài guǎngchǎng shàng, yǐnqǐle wéiguān zhě de zhùyì.
    - The crowd gathered in the square, attracting the attention of onlookers.
  - 市( )长(長)在( )大( )会(會)上( )向( )群( )众(眾)发(發)表( )了( )讲(講)话(話)。
    - Shìzhǎng zài dàhuì shàng xiàng qúnzhòng fābiǎo le jiǎnghuà.
    - The mayor delivered a speech to the multitude at the conference.
  - 为(為)了( )满(滿)足( )大( )众(眾)的( )需( )求( )，公( )司( )推( )出( )了( )新( )产(產)品( )。
    - Wèile mǎnzú dàzhòng de xūqiú, gōngsī tuīchū le xīn chǎnpǐn.
    - To meet the needs of the multitude, the company launched a new product.
